  const ProductsTab = () => {
    const filteredProducts = mockAdminProducts.filter(product => {
      const matchesSearch = product.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           product.seller.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || product.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedProducts = [...filteredProducts].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'price' || sortField === 'views' || sortField === 'sales') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleApproveProduct = (productId) => {
      alert(`Produit #${productId} approuvé`);
    };

    const handleRejectProduct = (productId) => {
      const reason = prompt('Raison du rejet:');
      if (reason) {
        alert(`Produit #${productId} rejeté: ${reason}`);
      }
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des produits</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
              />
              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="approved">Approuvés</option>
              <option value="pending">En attente</option>
              <option value="rejected">Rejetés</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Produit</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Vendeur</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'price' ? null : 'price')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Prix</span>
                      {sortField === 'price' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'dateAdded' ? null : 'dateAdded')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Date</span>
                      {sortField === 'dateAdded' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedProducts.map((product) => (
                  <tr key={product.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <img className="h-10 w-10 rounded object-cover" src={product.image} alt={product.name} />
                        <div className="ml-4">
                          <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{product.name}</div>
                          <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{product.category}</div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{product.seller}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">ID: {product.sellerId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatCurrency(product.price)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatDate(product.dateAdded)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(product.status)}`}>
                        {product.status === 'approved' && 'Approuvé'}
                        {product.status === 'pending' && 'En attente'}
                        {product.status === 'rejected' && 'Rejeté'}
                      </span>
                      {product.rejectionReason && (
                        <div className="text-xs text-red-600 mt-1">{product.rejectionReason}</div>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex space-x-2">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedProduct(product);
                            setShowProductModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900"
                        >
                          <Icons.Edit />
                        </button>
                        {product.status === 'pending' && (
                          <>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleApproveProduct(product.id)}
                              className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900"
                            >
                              <Icons.Check />
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleRejectProduct(product.id)}
                              className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900"
                            >
                              <Icons.X />
                            </button>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const UsersTab = () => {
    const filteredUsers = mockAdminUsers.filter(user => {
      const matchesSearch = user.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           user.email.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           user.phone.includes(searchQuery);
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || user.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedUsers = [...filteredUsers].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'totalSpent' || sortField === 'totalSales' || sortField === 'orders' || sortField === 'products') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleSuspendUser = (userId) => {
      const reason = prompt('Raison de la suspension:');
      if (reason) {
        alert(`Utilisateur #${userId} suspendu: ${reason}`);
      }
    };

    const handleActivateUser = (userId) => {
      alert(`Utilisateur #${userId} activé`);
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">

                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"

              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="active">Actifs</option>
              <option value="pending">En attente</option>

            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Utilisateur</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Rôle</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Localisation</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'totalSpent' ? null : 'totalSpent')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Dépenses</span>
                      {sortField === 'totalSpent' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>

                      {user.role === 'seller' && (

                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {user.location}

                      {user.role === 'customer' ? formatCurrency(user.totalSpent) : formatCurrency(user.totalSales)}

                        )}
                        {user.status === 'suspended' && (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => handleActivateUser(user.id)}
                            className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900"
                          >
                            <Icons.Check />
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const OrdersTab = () => {
    const filteredOrders = mockAdminOrders.filter(order => {
      const matchesSearch = order.orderId.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           order.customer.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           order.customerEmail.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || order.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedOrders = [...filteredOrders].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'total') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleUpdateStatus = (orderId, newStatus) => {
      alert(`Commande #${orderId} mise à jour: ${newStatus}`);
    };

    const handleProcessRefund = (orderId) => {
      const amount = prompt(`Montant du remboursement pour la commande #${orderId}:`);
      if (amount) {
        alert(`Remboursement de ${formatCurrency(amount)} effectué pour la commande #${orderId}`);
      }
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des commandes</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
              />
              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="pending">En attente</option>
              <option value="processing">En traitement</option>
              <option value="shipped">Expédiée</option>
              <option value="delivered">Livré</option>
              <option value="dispute">Litige</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Commande</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Client</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'total' ? null : 'total')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Total</span>
                      {sortField === 'total' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'date' ? null : 'date')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Date</span>
                      {sortField === 'date' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Méthode</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedOrders.map((order) => (
                  <tr key={order.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{order.orderId}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{order.items} article{order.items !== 1 ? 's' : ''}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{order.customer}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{order.customerEmail}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatCurrency(order.total)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatDate(order.date)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{order.paymentMethod}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(order.status)}`}>
                        {order.status === 'pending' && 'En attente'}
                        {order.status === 'processing' && 'En traitement'}
                        {order.status === 'shipped' && 'Expédiée'}
                        {order.status === 'delivered' && 'Livré'}
                        {order.status === 'dispute' && 'Litige'}
                      </span>
                      {order.disputeReason && (
                        <div className="text-xs text-orange-600 mt-1">{order.disputeReason}</div>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex flex-col space-y-1">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedOrder(order);
                            setShowOrderModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900 text-left"
                        >
                          Détails
                        </button>
                        {order.status === 'pending' && (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => handleUpdateStatus(order.id, 'processing')}
                            className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900 text-left"
                          >
                            Traiter
                          </button>
                        )}
                        {order.status === 'processing' && (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => handleUpdateStatus(order.id, 'shipped')}
                            className="text-purple-600 hover:text-purple-900 text-left"
                          >
                            Expédier
                          </button>
                        )}
                        {order.status === 'dispute' && (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => handleProcessRefund(order.id)}
                            className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900 text-left"
                          >
                            Rembourser
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const ReviewsTab = () => {
    const filteredReviews = mockAdminReviews.filter(review => {
      const matchesSearch = review.productName.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           review.customer.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           review.comment.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || review.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedReviews = [...filteredReviews].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'rating' || sortField === 'helpful') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleApproveReview = (reviewId) => {
      alert(`Avis #${reviewId} approuvé`);
    };

    const handleRejectReview = (reviewId) => {
      const reason = prompt('Raison du rejet:');
      if (reason) {
        alert(`Avis #${reviewId} rejeté: ${reason}`);
      }
    };

    const renderStars = (rating) => {
      return Array.from({ length: 5 }, (_, i) => (
        i < rating ? <Icons.Star key={i} /> : <Icons.StarEmpty key={i} />
      ));
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Modération des avis</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
              />
              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="approved">Approuvés</option>
              <option value="pending">En attente</option>
              <option value="flagged">Signalés</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Produit</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Client</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'rating' ? null : 'rating')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Note</span>
                      {sortField === 'rating' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'date' ? null : 'date')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Date</span>
                      {sortField === 'date' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Commentaire</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedReviews.map((review) => (
                  <tr key={review.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{review.productName}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">ID: {review.productId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{review.customer}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        {renderStars(review.rating)}
                        <span className="ml-2 text-sm text-gray-900">({review.rating})</span>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatDate(review.date)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900 line-clamp-2">{review.comment}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(review.status)}`}>
                        {review.status === 'approved' && 'Approuvé'}
                        {review.status === 'pending' && 'En attente'}
                        {review.status === 'flagged' && 'Signalé'}
                      </span>
                      {review.flagReason && (
                        <div className="text-xs text-red-600 mt-1">{review.flagReason}</div>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex flex-col space-y-1">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedReview(review);
                            setShowReviewModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900 text-left"
                        >
                          Détails
                        </button>
                        {review.status === 'pending' && (
                          <>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleApproveReview(review.id)}
                              className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900 text-left"
                            >
                              Approuver
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleRejectReview(review.id)}
                              className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900 text-left"
                            >
                              Rejeter
                            </button>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const SettingsTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Paramètres du système</h2>
      
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Paramètres généraux</h3>
        
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Nom du site</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              defaultValue="Jaay-ma"
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            />
          </div>
          
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Adresse email</label>
            <input
              type="email"
              defaultValue="contact@jaay-ma.sn"
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            />
          </div>
          
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Téléphone</label>
            <input
              type="tel"
              defaultValue="+221 77 123 45 67"
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            />
          </div>
          
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Adresse</label>
            <textarea
              rows={3}
              defaultValue="Avenue Cheikh Anta Diop, Dakar, Sénégal"
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            ></textarea>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end">
          <button className="bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium">
            Enregistrer les modifications
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Paramètres de paiement</h3>
        
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Orange Money</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Activer les paiements via Orange Money</p>
            </div>
            <button className="bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium">
              Activé
            </button>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Wave</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Activer les paiements via Wave</p>
            </div>
            <button className="bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium">
              Activé
            </button>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Cartes bancaires</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Activer les paiements par carte</p>
            </div>
            <button className="bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium">
              Activé
            </button>
          </div>
          
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Paiement à la livraison</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Activer le paiement à la livraison</p>
            </div>
            <button className="bg-green-500 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium">
              Activé
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Frais de livraison</h3>
        
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Zone Dakar</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                defaultValue="Gratuit"
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Autres régions</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                defaultValue="5000 XOF"
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Livraison express (même jour)</label>
            <input
              type="text"
              defaultValue="10000 XOF"
              className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end">
          <button className="bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium">
            Enregistrer les modifications
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const Sidebar = () => (
    <div className={`fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-50 w-64 bg-gray-900 text-white transform ${sidebarOpen ? 'translate-x-0' : '-translate-x-full'} transition-transform duration-300 ease-in-out lg:translate-x-0 lg:static lg:inset-0`}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between h-16 px-4 border-b border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mr-2">
            <span className="text-white font-bold text-sm">J</span>
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold">Jaay-ma Admin</span>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}
          className="lg:hidden"
        >
          <Icons.X />
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <nav className="mt-5 px-2">
        <div className="space-y-1">
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'dashboard' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Dashboard />
            <span className="ml-3">Tableau de bord</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('products')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'products' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Products />
            <span className="ml-3">Produits</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('users')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'users' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Users />
            <span className="ml-3">Utilisateurs</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('orders')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'orders' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Orders />
            <span className="ml-3">Commandes</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('reviews')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'reviews' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Reviews />
            <span className="ml-3">Avis</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('settings')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'settings' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Settings />
            <span className="ml-3">Paramètres</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </nav>
      
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 w-full p-4 border-t border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="h-8 w-8 bg-gray-300 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <Icons.User />
          </div>
          <div className="ml-3">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{currentUser?.role}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleLogout}
          className="mt-3 w-full bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded text-sm"
        >
          Déconnexion
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const renderActiveTab = () => {
    switch (activeTab) {
      case 'dashboard':
        return <DashboardTab />;
      case 'products':
        return <ProductsTab />;
      case 'users':
        return <UsersTab />;
      case 'orders':
        return <OrdersTab />;
      case 'reviews':
        return <ReviewsTab />;
      case 'settings':
        return <SettingsTab />;
      default:
        return <DashboardTab />;
    }
  };

  if (!currentUser || currentUser.role !== 'admin') {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow-lg max-w-md w-full">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
              <span className="text-white font-bold text-xl">J</span>
            </div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">Accès au panel administrateur</h2>
            <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6">Veuillez vous connecter avec un compte administrateur.</p>
            
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                <p><strong>Email:</strong> admin@jaay-ma.com</p>
                <p><strong>Mot de passe:</strong> n'importe lequel</p>
              </div>
              
              <input
                type="email"
                placeholder="Email"
                value={loginForm.email}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, email: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <input
                type="password"
                placeholder="Mot de passe"
                value={loginForm.password}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, password: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <button
                onClick={handleLogin}
                className="w-full bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded-lg font-medium"
              >
                Se connecter
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
      <Sidebar />
      
      <div className={`lg:ml-64 transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'lg:ml-64' : 'lg:ml-0'}`}>
        <header className="bg-white shadow-sm border-b border-gray-200">
          <div className="px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div className="flex items-center">
              <button
                onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
                className="lg:hidden p-2 rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100"
              >
                <Icons.Menu />
              </button>
              <h1 className="ml-2 text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">
                {activeTab === 'dashboard' && 'Tableau de bord'}
                {activeTab === 'products' && 'Gestion des produits'}
                {activeTab === 'users' && 'Gestion des utilisateurs'}
                {activeTab === 'orders' && 'Gestion des commandes'}
                {activeTab === 'reviews' && 'Modération des avis'}
                {activeTab === 'settings' && 'Paramètres du système'}
              </h1>
            </div>
            
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                Bienvenue, <span className="font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</span>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={handleLogout}
                className="text-sm text-red-600 hover:text-red-800"
              >
                Déconnexion
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>
        
        <main className="px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
          {renderActiveTab()}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;

// App Component
const App = () => {
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState(null);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(true);
  const [showLoginModal, setShowLoginModal] = useState(false);
  const [loginForm, setLoginForm] = useState({ email: '', password: '' });
  const [selectedProduct, setSelectedProduct] = useState(null);
  const [selectedUser, setSelectedUser] = useState(null);
  const [selectedOrder, setSelectedOrder] = useState(null);
  const [selectedReview, setSelectedReview] = useState(null);
  const [showProductModal, setShowProductModal] = useState(false);
  const [showUserModal, setShowUserModal] = useState(false);
  const [showOrderModal, setShowOrderModal] = useState(false);
  const [showReviewModal, setShowReviewModal] = useState(false);
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState('all');
  const [sortField, setSortField] = useState('date');
  const [sortDirection, setSortDirection] = useState('desc');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate admin login
    const savedUser = localStorage.getItem('jaayma-user');
    if (savedUser) {
      const user = JSON.parse(savedUser);
      if (user.role === 'admin') {
        setCurrentUser(user);
      } else {
        // Force admin login for demo
        const adminUser = {
          id: 3,
          name: "Administrateur",
          email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
          role: "admin",
          location: "Dakar"
        };
        setCurrentUser(adminUser);
        localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      }
    } else {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
    }
  }, []);

  const handleLogin = () => {
    if (loginForm.email === 'admin@jaay-ma.com') {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      setShowLoginModal(false);
      setLoginForm({ email: '', password: '' });
    } else {
      alert('Utilisez admin@jaay-ma.com pour accéder au panel administrateur');
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setCurrentUser(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('jaayma-user');
    window.location.href = '/'; // Redirect to main site
  };

  const formatCurrency = (amount) => {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('fr-SN', {
      style: 'currency',
      currency: 'XOF',
      minimumFractionDigits: 0
    }).format(amount);
  };

  const formatDate = (dateString) => {
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('fr-SN');
  };

  const getBadgeColor = (status) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'approved': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'pending': return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
      case 'rejected': return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
      case 'active': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'suspended': return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
      case 'pending': return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
      case 'processing': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
      case 'shipped': return 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-800';
      case 'delivered': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'dispute': return 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-800';
      default: return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
    }
  };

  // Admin Panel Components
  const DashboardTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-blue-100 text-blue-600">
              <Icons.Dashboard />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Ventes aujourd'hui</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{formatCurrency(mockAdminData.sales.today)}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex items-center text-sm">
            <span className="text-green-500 font-medium">+{mockAdminData.sales.growth}%</span>
            <span className="text-gray-500 ml-2">vs hier</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-600">
              <Icons.Products />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Produits</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockAdminData.products.total}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-yellow-600">{mockAdminData.products.pending} en attente</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">

              <Icons.Orders />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Commandes</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockAdminData.orders.total}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-red-600">{mockAdminData.orders.pending} en attente</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Charts and Analytics */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Ventes hebdomadaires</h3>
          <div className="h-64 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📊</div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Graphique des ventes hebdomadaires</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Répartition par catégorie</h3>

              </div>

              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Nouvel utilisateur inscrit</p>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Moussa Diallo - 15 janv. 2024</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center">
              <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-orange-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Commande en attente</p>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">JM1001 - 15 janv. 2024</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center">
              <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-red-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Produit rejeté</p>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Sac à Main en Cuir Artisanal - 14 janv. 2024</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const ProductsTab = () => {
    const filteredProducts = mockAdminProducts.filter(product => {
      const matchesSearch = product.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           product.seller.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || product.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedProducts = [...filteredProducts].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'price' || sortField === 'views' || sortField === 'sales') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleApproveProduct = (productId) => {
      alert(`Produit #${productId} approuvé`);
    };

    const handleRejectProduct = (productId) => {
      const reason = prompt('Raison du rejet:');
      if (reason) {
        alert(`Produit #${productId} rejeté: ${reason}`);
      }
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des produits</h2>

              />

                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="approved">Approuvés</option>
              <option value="pending">En attente</option>
              <option value="rejected">Rejetés</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Produit</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Vendeur</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'price' ? null : 'price')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Prix</span>
                      {sortField === 'price' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'dateAdded' ? null : 'dateAdded')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Date</span>
                      {sortField === 'dateAdded' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedProducts.map((product) => (
                  <tr key={product.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <img className="h-10 w-10 rounded object-cover" src={product.image} alt={product.name} />
                        <div className="ml-4">
                          <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{product.name}</div>
                          <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{product.category}</div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{product.seller}</div>
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">ID: {product.sellerId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatCurrency(product.price)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatDate(product.dateAdded)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(product.status)}`}>
                        {product.status === 'approved' && 'Approuvé'}
                        {product.status === 'pending' && 'En attente'}
                        {product.status === 'rejected' && 'Rejeté'}
                      </span>
                      {product.rejectionReason && (
                        <div className="text-xs text-red-600 mt-1">{product.rejectionReason}</div>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex space-x-2">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedProduct(product);
                            setShowProductModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900"
                        >
                          <Icons.Edit />
                        </button>
                        {product.status === 'pending' && (
                          <>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleApproveProduct(product.id)}
                              className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900"
                            >
                              <Icons.Check />
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleRejectProduct(product.id)}
                              className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900"
                            >
                              <Icons.X />
                            </button>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const UsersTab = () => {
    const filteredUsers = mockAdminUsers.filter(user => {
      const matchesSearch = user.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           user.email.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           user.phone.includes(searchQuery);
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || user.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedUsers = [...filteredUsers].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'totalSpent' || sortField === 'totalSales' || sortField === 'orders' || sortField === 'products') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const handleSuspendUser = (userId) => {
      const reason = prompt('Raison de la suspension:');
      if (reason) {
        alert(`Utilisateur #${userId} suspendu: ${reason}`);
      }
    };

    const handleActivateUser = (userId) => {
      alert(`Utilisateur #${userId} activé`);
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des utilisateurs</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
