// App Component
const App = () => {
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState(null);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(true);
  const [showLoginModal, setShowLoginModal] = useState(false);
  const [loginForm, setLoginForm] = useState({ email: '', password: '' });
  const [selectedDelivery, setSelectedDelivery] = useState(null);
  const [selectedCourier, setSelectedCourier] = useState(null);
  const [selectedPickup, setSelectedPickup] = useState(null);
  const [selectedZone, setSelectedZone] = useState(null);
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState('all');
  const [sortField, setSortField] = useState('estimatedTime');
  const [sortDirection, setSortDirection] = useState('asc');
  const [showScheduleModal, setShowScheduleModal] = useState(false);
  const [scheduleData, setScheduleData] = useState({
    orderId: '',
    date: '',
    timeSlot: '',
    deliveryType: 'standard'
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate admin login
    const savedUser = localStorage.getItem('jaayma-user');
    if (savedUser) {
      const user = JSON.parse(savedUser);
      if (user.role === 'admin') {
        setCurrentUser(user);
      } else {
        // Force admin login for demo
        const adminUser = {
          id: 3,
          name: "Administrateur",
          email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
          role: "admin",
          location: "Dakar"
        };
        setCurrentUser(adminUser);
        localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      }
    } else {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
    }
  }, []);

  const handleLogin = () => {
    if (loginForm.email === 'admin@jaay-ma.com') {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      setShowLoginModal(false);
      setLoginForm({ email: '', password: '' });
    } else {
      alert('Utilisez admin@jaay-ma.com pour accéder au panel administrateur');
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setCurrentUser(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('jaayma-user');
    window.location.href = '/'; // Redirect to main site
  };

  const formatCurrency = (amount) => {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('fr-SN', {
      style: 'currency',
      currency: 'XOF',
      minimumFractionDigits: 0
    }).format(amount);
  };

  const formatDate = (dateString) => {
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('fr-SN');
  };

  const getBadgeColor = (status) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'in_transit': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
      case 'scheduled': return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
      case 'delivered': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'delayed': return 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-800';
      case 'active': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      case 'inactive': return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
      default: return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
    }
  };

  const getProgressColor = (progress) => {
    if (progress < 30) return 'bg-red-500';
    if (progress < 70) return 'bg-yellow-500';
    return 'bg-green-500';
  };

  // Logistics Panel Components
  const DashboardTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-blue-100 text-blue-600">
              <Icons.Truck />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Livraisons totales</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockLogisticsData.deliveryStats.totalDeliveries}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex items-center text-sm">
            <span className="text-green-500 font-medium">+12.5%</span>
            <span className="text-gray-500 ml-2">vs mois dernier</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-600">
              <Icons.Check />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Taux de livraison à l'heure</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockLogisticsData.deliveryStats.onTimeRate}%</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-blue-600">Objectif: 95%</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-purple-100 text-purple-600">
              <Icons.Clock />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Délai moyen de livraison</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockLogisticsData.deliveryStats.averageDeliveryTime} jours</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-red-600">-0.2 jours</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-orange-100 text-orange-600">
              <Icons.Users />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Livreur(s) actif(s)</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockLogisticsData.deliveryStats.activeCouriers}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-gray-600">Sur 50 total</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Charts and Analytics */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Livraisons par zone</h3>
          <div className="h-64 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📊</div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Graphique des livraisons par zone</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Performance des livreurs</h3>
          <div className="h-64 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📈</div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Graphique de performance des livreurs</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Recent Deliveries */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow">
        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Livraisons récentes</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="p-6">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {mockLogisticsData.deliveries.slice(0, 4).map((delivery) => (
              <div key={delivery.id} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <div className="flex items-center">
                  <div className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-full ${getProgressColor(delivery.progress)} mr-3`}></div>
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{delivery.orderId} - {delivery.customer}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{delivery.address}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(delivery.status)}`}>
                    {delivery.status === 'in_transit' && 'En transit'}
                    {delivery.status === 'scheduled' && 'Programmée'}
                    {delivery.status === 'delivered' && 'Livré'}
                  </span>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">À {delivery.estimatedTime}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const DeliveriesTab = () => {
    const filteredDeliveries = mockLogisticsData.deliveries.filter(delivery => {
      const matchesSearch = delivery.orderId.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           delivery.customer.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || delivery.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedDeliveries = [...filteredDeliveries].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'progress') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const updateDeliveryStatus = (deliveryId, newStatus) => {
      alert(`Statut de la livraison #${deliveryId} mis à jour: ${newStatus}`);
    };

    const assignCourier = (deliveryId, courierId) => {
      const courier = mockLogisticsData.couriers.find(c => c.id === courierId);
      if (courier) {
        alert(`Livraison #${deliveryId} assignée à ${courier.name}`);
      }
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des livraisons</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
              />
              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="scheduled">Programmées</option>
              <option value="in_transit">En transit</option>
              <option value="delivered">Livré</option>
              <option value="delayed">Retard</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Commande</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Client</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'estimatedTime' ? null : 'estimatedTime')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Heure estimée</span>
                      {sortField === 'estimatedTime' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Lieu</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'progress' ? null : 'progress')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Progression</span>
                      {sortField === 'progress' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedDeliveries.map((delivery) => (
                  <tr key={delivery.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{delivery.orderId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{delivery.customer}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {delivery.estimatedTime}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900 line-clamp-2">{delivery.address}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2.5 mr-2">
                          <div 
                            className={`h-2.5 rounded-full ${getProgressColor(delivery.progress)}`} 
                            style={{ width: `${delivery.progress}%` }}
                          ></div>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{delivery.progress}%</span>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(delivery.status)}`}>
                        {delivery.status === 'in_transit' && 'En transit'}
                        {delivery.status === 'scheduled' && 'Programmée'}
                        {delivery.status === 'delivered' && 'Livré'}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex flex-col space-y-1">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedDelivery(delivery);
                            setShowScheduleModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900 text-left"
                        >
                          Suivi GPS
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(delivery.id, 'delivered')}
                          className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900 text-left"
                        >
                          Marquer comme livré
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const CouriersTab = () => {
    const filteredCouriers = mockLogisticsData.couriers.filter(courier => {
      const matchesSearch = courier.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
                           courier.phone.includes(searchQuery);
      const matchesStatus = filterStatus === 'all' || courier.status === filterStatus;
      return matchesSearch && matchesStatus;
    });

    const sortedCouriers = [...filteredCouriers].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'deliveriesToday' || sortField === 'rating') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const activateCourier = (courierId) => {
      alert(`Livreur #${courierId} activé`);
    };

    const deactivateCourier = (courierId) => {
      alert(`Livreur #${courierId} désactivé`);
    };

    const renderStars = (rating) => {
      return Array.from({ length: 5 }, (_, i) => (
        i < rating ? <Icons.Star key={i} /> : <Icons.StarEmpty key={i} />
      ));
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Gestion des livreurs</h2>
          <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 w-full sm:w-auto">
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                placeholder="Rechercher..."
                value={searchQuery}
                onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
                className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
              />
              <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
                <Icons.Search />
              </div>
            </div>
            <select
              value={filterStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setFilterStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
            >
              <option value="all">Tous les statuts</option>
              <option value="active">Actifs</option>
              <option value="inactive">Inactifs</option>
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Livreur</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Contact</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Véhicule</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'deliveriesToday' ? null : 'deliveriesToday')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Livraisons aujourd'hui</span>
                      {sortField === 'deliveriesToday' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'rating' ? null : 'rating')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Note</span>
                      {sortField === 'rating' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedCouriers.map((courier) => (
                  <tr key={courier.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        <div className="h-10 w-10 bg-gray-300 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                          <Icons.User />
                        </div>
                        <div className="ml-4">
                          <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{courier.name}</div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{courier.phone}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {courier.vehicle}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {courier.deliveriesToday}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="flex items-center">
                        {renderStars(courier.rating)}
                        <span className="ml-2 text-sm text-gray-900">({courier.rating})</span>
                      </div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(courier.status)}`}>
                        {courier.status === 'active' && 'Actif'}
                        {courier.status === 'inactive' && 'Inactif'}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <div className="flex flex-col space-y-1">
                        <button
                          onClick={() => {
                            setSelectedCourier(courier);
                            setShowScheduleModal(true);
                          }}
                          className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900 text-left"
                        >
                          Localisation
                        </button>
                        {courier.status === 'active' ? (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => deactivateCourier(courier.id)}
                            className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900 text-left"
                          >
                            Désactiver
                          </button>
                        ) : (
                          <button
                            onClick={() => activateCourier(courier.id)}
                            className="text-green-600 hover:text-green-900 text-left"
                          >
                            Activer
                          </button>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const ZonesTab = () => {
    const filteredZones = mockLogisticsData.zones.filter(zone => {
      return zone.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
             zone.coverage.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
    });

    const sortedZones = [...filteredZones].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortField === 'cost') {
        aValue = parseFloat(aValue.replace(/[^\d]/g, ''));
        bValue = parseFloat(bValue.replace(/[^\d]/g, ''));
      }
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Zones de livraison</h2>
          <div className="relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Rechercher..."
              value={searchQuery}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
              className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
            />
            <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
              <Icons.Search />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Zone</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Couverture</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'deliveryTime' ? null : 'deliveryTime')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Délai de livraison</span>
                      {sortField === 'deliveryTime' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">
                    <button 
                      onClick={() => setSortField(sortField === 'cost' ? null : 'cost')}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-1"
                    >
                      <span>Frais de livraison</span>
                      {sortField === 'cost' && (
                        <span>{sortDirection === 'asc' ? '↑' : '↓'}</span>
                      )}
                    </button>
                  </th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Livraison express</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {sortedZones.map((zone) => (
                  <tr key={zone.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{zone.name}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{zone.coverage}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {zone.deliveryTime}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {zone.cost}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      {zone.expressAvailable ? (
                        <span className="px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-800">
                          Disponible ({zone.expressCost})
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full bg-red-100 text-red-800">
                          Non disponible
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const PickupPointsTab = () => {
    const filteredPickupPoints = mockLogisticsData.pickupPoints.filter(point => {
      return point.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
             point.address.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
    });

    const sortedPickupPoints = [...filteredPickupPoints].sort((a, b) => {
      return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
    });

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Points de retrait (Click & Collect)</h2>
          <div className="relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Rechercher..."
              value={searchQuery}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
              className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
            />
            <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
              <Icons.Search />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {sortedPickupPoints.map((point) => (
            <div key={point.id} className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
              <div className="flex items-start">
                <div className="p-2 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg mr-3">
                  <Icons.Location />
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">{point.name}</h3>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">{point.address}</p>
                  <div className="mt-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500">
                      <Icons.Clock className="mr-1" />
                      <span>Horaires: {point.hours}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
                      <Icons.Phone className="mr-1" />
                      <span>{point.phone}</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
                <button
                  onClick={() => {
                    setSelectedPickup(point);
                    setShowScheduleModal(true);
                  }}
                  className="w-full bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium"
                >
                  Voir sur la carte
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const ScheduleTab = () => {
    const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([
      { id: 1, orderId: "JM1001", customer: "Fatou Diop", time: "08:00", status: "scheduled" },
      { id: 2, orderId: "JM1002", customer: "Aliou Sow", time: "09:30", status: "scheduled" },
      { id: 3, orderId: "JM1003", customer: "Moussa Diallo", time: "11:00", status: "scheduled" },
      { id: 4, orderId: "JM1004", customer: "Awa Ba", time: "14:00", status: "scheduled" },
      { id: 5, orderId: "JM1005", customer: "Fatou Diop", time: "16:30", status: "scheduled" }
    ]);

    const timeSlots = [
      "08:00 - 10:00", "10:00 - 12:00", "14:00 - 16:00", "16:00 - 18:00"
    ];

    const handleScheduleDelivery = (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      alert(`Livraison programmée pour ${scheduleData.date} à ${scheduleData.timeSlot}`);
      setShowScheduleModal(false);
      setScheduleData({ orderId: '', date: '', timeSlot: '', deliveryType: 'standard' });
    };

    const updateDeliveryTime = (deliveryId, newTime) => {
      setDeliveries(prev => prev.map(delivery => 
        delivery.id === deliveryId ? { ...delivery, time: newTime } : delivery
      ));
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Programmation des livraisons</h2>
          <button
            onClick={() => setShowScheduleModal(true)}
            className="bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium"
          >
            Programmer une livraison
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">
                <tr>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Commande</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Client</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Heure</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Type</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {deliveries.map((delivery) => (
                  <tr key={delivery.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{delivery.orderId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{delivery.customer}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <select
                        value={delivery.time}
                        onChange={(e) => updateDeliveryTime(delivery.id, e.target.value)}
                        className="text-sm border border-gray-300 rounded px-2 py-1"
                      >
                        {timeSlots.map(slot => (
                          <option key={slot} value={slot}>{slot}</option>
                        ))}
                      </select>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className="px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-800">
                        Standard
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <button
                        onClick={() => {
                          const updatedDeliveries = deliveries.filter(d => d.id !== delivery.id);
                          setDeliveries(updatedDeliveries);
                        }}
                        className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-900"
                      >
                        <Icons.X />
                      </button>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Calendar view */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Calendrier des livraisons</h3>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-1">
            {['Lun', 'Mar', 'Mer', 'Jeu', 'Ven', 'Sam', 'Dim'].map(day => (
              <div key={day} className="p-2 text-center font-medium text-gray-600">
                {day}
              </div>
            ))}
            {Array.from({ length: 35 }, (_, i) => {
              const date = i + 1;
              const hasDelivery = [5, 8, 12, 15, 18, 22, 25, 28].includes(date);
              return (
                <div key={i} className={`p-2 text-center border ${hasDelivery ? 'bg-blue-50 border-blue-200' : 'border-gray-200'}`}>
                  <div className="text-sm">{date}</div>
                  {hasDelivery && (
                    <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-blue-500 rounded-full mx-auto mt-1"></div>
                  )}
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Schedule Modal */}
        {showScheduleModal && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 z-50">
            <div className="bg-white rounded-lg max-w-md w-full p-6">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
                <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">Programmer une livraison</h3>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setShowScheduleModal(false)}
                  className="p-2 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-full"
                >
                  <Icons.X />
                </button>
              </div>
              
              <form onSubmit={handleScheduleDelivery}>
                <div className="space-y-4">
                  <div>
                    <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Numéro de commande</label>
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      value={scheduleData.orderId}
                      onChange={(e) => setScheduleData({...scheduleData, orderId: e.target.value})}
                      className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                      required
                    />
                  </div>
                  
                  <div>
                    <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Date de livraison</label>
                    <input
                      type="date"
                      value={scheduleData.date}
                      onChange={(e) => setScheduleData({...scheduleData, date: e.target.value})}
                      className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                      required
                    />
                  </div>
                  
                  <div>
                    <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Créneau horaire</label>
                    <select
                      value={scheduleData.timeSlot}
                      onChange={(e) => setScheduleData({...scheduleData, timeSlot: e.target.value})}
                      className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                      required
                    >
                      <option value="">Sélectionner un créneau</option>
                      {timeSlots.map(slot => (
                        <option key={slot} value={slot}>{slot}</option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                  </div>
                  
                  <div>
                    <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">Type de livraison</label>
                    <select
                      value={scheduleData.deliveryType}
                      onChange={(e) => setScheduleData({...scheduleData, deliveryType: e.target.value})}
                      className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
                    >
                      <option value="standard">Standard</option>
                      <option value="express">Express (même jour)</option>
                    </select>
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                <div className="mt-6 flex justify-end space-x-3">
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setShowScheduleModal(false)}
                    className="px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50"
                  >
                    Annuler
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="submit"
                    className="px-4 py-2 bg-blue-500 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-600"
                  >
                    Programmer
                  </button>
                </div>
              </form>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  };

  const Sidebar = () => (
    <div className={`fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-50 w-64 bg-gray-900 text-white transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'translate-x-0' : '-translate-x-full'} lg:translate-x-0 lg:static lg:inset-0`}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between h-16 px-4 border-b border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mr-2">
            <span className="text-white font-bold text-sm">J</span>
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold">Jaay-ma Logistique</span>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}
          className="lg:hidden"
        >
          <Icons.X />
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <nav className="mt-5 px-2">
        <div className="space-y-1">
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'dashboard' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Dashboard />
            <span className="ml-3">Tableau de bord</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('deliveries')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'deliveries' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Truck />
            <span className="ml-3">Livraisons</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('couriers')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'couriers' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Users />
            <span className="ml-3">Livreurs</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('zones')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'zones' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Map />
            <span className="ml-3">Zones</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('pickup')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'pickup' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Location />
            <span className="ml-3">Points de retrait</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveTab('schedule')}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              activeTab === 'schedule' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Calendar />
            <span className="ml-3">Programmation</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </nav>
      
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 w-full p-4 border-t border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="h-8 w-8 bg-gray-300 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <Icons.User />
          </div>
          <div className="ml-3">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{currentUser?.role}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleLogout}
          className="mt-3 w-full bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded text-sm"
        >
          Déconnexion
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  const renderActiveTab = () => {
    switch (activeTab) {
      case 'dashboard':
        return <DashboardTab />;
      case 'deliveries':
        return <DeliveriesTab />;
      case 'couriers':
        return <CouriersTab />;
      case 'zones':
        return <ZonesTab />;
      case 'pickup':
        return <PickupPointsTab />;
      case 'schedule':
        return <ScheduleTab />;
      default:
        return <DashboardTab />;
    }
  };

  if (!currentUser || currentUser.role !== 'admin') {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow-lg max-w-md w-full">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
              <span className="text-white font-bold text-xl">J</span>
            </div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">Accès au panel logistique</h2>
            <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6">Veuillez vous connecter avec un compte administrateur.</p>
            
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                <p><strong>Email:</strong> admin@jaay-ma.com</p>
                <p><strong>Mot de passe:</strong> n'importe lequel</p>
              </div>
              
              <input
                type="email"
                placeholder="Email"
                value={loginForm.email}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, email: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <input
                type="password"
                placeholder="Mot de passe"
                value={loginForm.password}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, password: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <button
                onClick={handleLogin}
                className="w-full bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded-lg font-medium"
              >
                Se connecter
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
      <Sidebar />
      
      <div className={`transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'lg:ml-64' : 'lg:ml-0'} min-h-screen`}>
        <header className="bg-white shadow-sm border-b border-gray-200">
          <div className="px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div className="flex items-center">
              <button
                onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
                className="lg:hidden p-2 rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100"
              >
                <Icons.Menu />
              </button>
              <h1 className="ml-2 text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">
                {activeTab === 'dashboard' && 'Tableau de bord logistique'}
                {activeTab === 'deliveries' && 'Gestion des livraisons'}
                {activeTab === 'couriers' && 'Gestion des livreurs'}
                {activeTab === 'zones' && 'Zones de livraison'}
                {activeTab === 'pickup' && 'Points de retrait'}
                {activeTab === 'schedule' && 'Programmation des livraisons'}
              </h1>
            </div>
            
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                Bienvenue, <span className="font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</span>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={handleLogout}
                className="text-sm text-red-600 hover:text-red-800"
              >
                Déconnexion
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>
        
        <main className="px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 min-h-screen">
          {renderActiveTab()}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;

  Instagram: () => <svg className="w-5 h-5" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M12.017 0C8.827 0 8.32 0.013 7.053 0.072 5.739 0.132 4.896 0.306 4.083 // App Component
const App = () => {
  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState(null);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(true);
  const [showLoginModal, setShowLoginModal] = useState(false);
  const [loginForm, setLoginForm] = useState({ email: '', password: '' });
  const [selectedFeature, setSelectedFeature] = useState(null);
  const [showConfigModal, setShowConfigModal] = useState(false);
  const [configData, setConfigData] = useState({});
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState('all');
  const [sortField, setSortField] = useState('revenueGenerated');
  const [sortDirection, setSortDirection] = useState('desc');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate admin login
    const savedUser = localStorage.getItem('jaayma-user');
    if (savedUser) {
      const user = JSON.parse(savedUser);
      if (user.role === 'admin') {
        setCurrentUser(user);
      } else {
        // Force admin login for demo
        const adminUser = {
          id: 3,
          name: "Administrateur",
          email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
          role: "admin",
          location: "Dakar"
        };
        setCurrentUser(adminUser);
        localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      }
    } else {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
    }
  }, []);

  const handleLogin = () => {
    if (loginForm.email === 'admin@jaay-ma.com') {
      const adminUser = {
        id: 3,
        name: "Administrateur",
        email: "admin@jaay-ma.com",
        role: "admin",
        location: "Dakar"
      };
      setCurrentUser(adminUser);
      localStorage.setItem('jaayma-user', JSON.stringify(adminUser));
      setShowLoginModal(false);
      setLoginForm({ email: '', password: '' });
    } else {
      alert('Utilisez admin@jaay-ma.com pour accéder au panel administrateur');
    }
  };

  const handleLogout = () => {
    setCurrentUser(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('jaayma-user');
    window.location.href = '/'; // Redirect to main site
  };

  const formatCurrency = (amount) => {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('fr-SN', {
      style: 'currency',
      currency: 'XOF',
      minimumFractionDigits: 0
    }).format(amount);
  };

  const formatDate = (dateString) => {
    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('fr-SN');
  };

  const getBadgeColor = (value) => {
    if (value > 90) return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
    if (value > 70) return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
    if (value > 50) return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
    return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
  };

  const formatPercentage = (value) => {
    return `${value}%`;
  };

  // Advanced Features Panel Components
  const DashboardTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-blue-100 text-blue-600">
              <Icons.Chart />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Taux de conversion</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockAdvancedData.analytics.conversionRate}%</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex items-center text-sm">
            <span className="text-green-500 font-medium">+2.3%</span>
            <span className="text-gray-500 ml-2">vs mois dernier</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
          <div className="flex items-center">
            <div className="p-3 rounded-full bg-green-100 text-green-600">
              <Icons.Gift />
            </div>
            <div className="ml-4">
              <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600">Membres fidélité</p>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{mockAdvancedData.loyalty.totalMembers}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-gray-500">
            <span className="text-blue-600">Taux de rétention: {mockAdvancedData.loyalty.retentionRate}%</span>
          </div>
        </div>

  const AIRecommendationsTab = () => {
    const filteredRecommendations = mockAdvancedData.recommendations.topCategories.filter(category => {
      return category.category.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
    });

    const sortedRecommendations = [...filteredRecommendations].sort((a, b) => {
      let aValue = a[sortField];
      let bValue = b[sortField];
      
      if (sortDirection === 'asc') {
        return aValue > bValue ? 1 : -1;
      } else {
        return aValue < bValue ? 1 : -1;
      }
    });

    const updateRecommendationSettings = (category, settings) => {
      alert(`Paramètres de recommandation mis à jour pour ${category}`);
    };

  const FraudDetectionTab = () => {
    const [suspiciousTransactions, setSuspiciousTransactions] = useState([
      {
        id: 1,
        orderId: "JM1001",
        customer: "Fatou Diop",
        amount: 350000,
        riskScore: 95,
        detectedRule: "Montant élevé + nouvelle carte",
        status: "flagged",
        timestamp: "2024-01-15 14:30:25"
      },
      {
        id: 2,
        orderId: "JM1002",
        customer: "Aliou Sow",
        amount: 180000,
        riskScore: 88,
        detectedRule: "Adresse IP différente",
        status: "flagged",
        timestamp: "2024-01-15 13:15:42"
      },
      {
        id: 3,
        orderId: "JM1003",
        customer: "Moussa Diallo",
        amount: 25000,
        riskScore: 45,
        detectedRule: "Achat multiple en peu de temps",
        status: "cleared",
        timestamp: "2024-01-15 12:45:18"
      }
    ]);

    const handleReviewTransaction = (transactionId) => {
      const action = prompt('Action à prendre (approve/reject):');
      if (action === 'approve') {
        setSuspiciousTransactions(prev => prev.map(t => 
          t.id === transactionId ? { ...t, status: 'approved' } : t
        ));
      } else if (action === 'reject') {
        const reason = prompt('Raison du rejet:');
        setSuspiciousTransactions(prev => prev.map(t => 
          t.id === transactionId ? { ...t, status: 'rejected', rejectionReason: reason } : t
        ));
      }
    };

    const getRiskColor = (score) => {
      if (score >= 90) return 'bg-red-100 text-red-800';
      if (score >= 70) return 'bg-orange-100 text-orange-800';
      if (score >= 50) return 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800';
      return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Détection de fraude</h2>
            <p className="text-gray-600 mt-1">Transactions détectées: {mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.flaggedTransactions} • Taux de détection: {formatPercentage(mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.detectionRate)}%</p>
          </div>
          <div className="relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Rechercher..."
              value={searchQuery}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
              className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
            />
            <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
              <Icons.Search />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Statistiques</h3>
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-gray-600">Transactions totales:</span>
                <span className="font-semibold">{mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.totalTransactions}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-gray-600">Transactions suspectes:</span>
                <span className="font-semibold text-red-600">{mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.flaggedTransactions}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-gray-600">Taux de détection:</span>
                <span className="font-semibold text-green-600">{formatPercentage(mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.detectionRate)}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-gray-600">Faux positifs:</span>
                <span className="font-semibold text-yellow-600">{mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.falsePositives}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between">
                <span className="text-gray-600">Pertes évitées:</span>
                <span className="font-semibold">{formatCurrency(mockAdvancedData.fraudDetection.preventedLosses)}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Règles de détection</h3>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
                <span className="text-sm">Montant élevé pour le client</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
                <span className="text-sm">Adresse IP différente de l'habitude</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
                <span className="text-sm">Plusieurs achats en peu de temps</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
                <span className="text-sm">Nouvelle méthode de paiement</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full mr-3"></div>
                <span className="text-sm">Adresse de livraison différente</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Performance</h3>
            <div className="h-40 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
              <div className="text-center">
                <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📈</div>
                <p className="text-gray-500">Taux de détection vs faux positifs</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow overflow-hidden">
          <div className="overflow-x-auto">
            <table className="min-w-full divide-y divide-gray-200">
              <thead className="bg-gray-50">

                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Commande</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Client</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Montant</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Score de risque</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Règle détectée</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Statut</th>
                  <th className="px-6 py-3 text-left text-xs font-medium text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Actions</th>
                </tr>
              </thead>
              <tbody className="bg-white divide-y divide-gray-200">
                {suspiciousTransactions.map((transaction) => (
                  <tr key={transaction.id} className="hover:bg-gray-50">
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{transaction.orderId}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900">{transaction.customer}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm text-gray-900">
                      {formatCurrency(transaction.amount)}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${getRiskColor(transaction.riskScore)}`}>
                        {transaction.riskScore}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4">
                      <div className="text-sm text-gray-900 line-clamp-2">{transaction.detectedRule}</div>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap">
                      <span className={`px-2 inline-flex text-xs leading-5 font-semibold rounded-full ${
                        transaction.status === 'flagged' ? 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800' :
                        transaction.status === 'approved' ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-800' :
                        'bg-red-100 text-red-800'
                      }`}>
                        {transaction.status === 'flagged' && 'En attente'}
                        {transaction.status === 'approved' && 'Approuvé'}
                        {transaction.status === 'rejected' && 'Rejeté'}
                      </span>
                      {transaction.rejectionReason && (
                        <div className="text-xs text-red-600 mt-1">{transaction.rejectionReason}</div>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-6 py-4 whitespace-nowrap text-sm font-medium">
                      <button
                        onClick={() => handleReviewTransaction(transaction.id)}
                        className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-900"
                      >
                        Examiner
                      </button>
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                ))}
              </tbody>
            </table>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const InventoryAnalyticsTab = () => {

      {

        category: "Électronique",
        currentStock: 45,
        predictedDemand: 60,

      },
      {

        predictedDemand: 35,
        confidence: 88,
        action: "reorder"
      },
      {

        product: "Machine à Laver Samsung 8kg",
        category: "Électroménager",
        currentStock: 8,
        predictedDemand: 5,
        confidence: 75,
        action: "monitor"
      },
      {
        id: 4,
        product: "Sac à Main en Cuir Artisanal",
        category: "Mode",
        currentStock: 2,
        predictedDemand: 20,
        confidence: 95,
        action: "reorder"
      }
    ]);

    const handleUpdatePrediction = (predictionId, newAction) => {
      setPredictions(prev => prev.map(p => 
        p.id === predictionId ? { ...p, action: newAction } : p
      ));
    };

    return (
      <div className="space-y-6">

          </div>
          <div className="relative">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="Rechercher..."

        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
      <Sidebar />
      
      <div className={`transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'lg:ml-64' : 'lg:ml-0'} min-h-screen`}>
        <header className="bg-white shadow-sm border-b border-gray-200">
          <div className="px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div className="flex items-center">
              <button
                onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
                className="lg:hidden p-2 rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100"
              >
                <Icons.Menu />
              </button>
              <h1 className="ml-2 text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">
                {activeTab === 'dashboard' && 'Tableau de bord avancé'}
                {activeTab === 'ai' && 'Intelligence Artificielle'}
                {activeTab === 'marketing' && 'Marketing'}
                {activeTab === 'analytics' && 'Analytics'}
              </h1>
            </div>
            
            <div className="flex items-center space-x-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                Bienvenue, <span className="font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</span>
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={handleLogout}
                className="text-sm text-red-600 hover:text-red-800"
              >
                Déconnexion
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </header>
        
        <main className="px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 min-h-screen">
          {renderActiveTab()}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
