    </div>
  );

  // Logistique & Livraison
  const LogisticsTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Logistique & Livraison</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mt-1">Système de livraison optimisé pour le Sénégal</p>
        </div>
        <div className="relative">
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Rechercher..."
            value={searchQuery}
            onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
            className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
          />
          <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
            <Icons.Search />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Zones de livraison</h3>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {mockData.deliveryZones.map((zone) => (
              <div key={zone.id} className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                  <div>
                    <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">{zone.name}</h4>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">{zone.coverage}</p>
                  </div>
                  <span className={`px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(zone.expressAvailable ? 'active' : 'inactive')}`}>
                    {zone.expressAvailable ? 'Express' : 'Standard'}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Délai:</span>
                    <span className="ml-2 font-medium">{zone.deliveryTime}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Frais:</span>
                    <span className="ml-2 font-medium">{zone.cost}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                {zone.expressCost && (
                  <div className="mt-2 text-sm">
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Express:</span>
                    <span className="ml-2 font-medium">{zone.expressCost}</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Points de retrait (Click & Collect)</h3>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {mockData.pickupPoints.map((point) => (
              <div key={point.id} className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                <div className="flex items-start">
                  <div className="p-2 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg mr-3">
                    <Icons.Location />
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1">
                    <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">{point.name}</h4>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">{point.address}</p>
                    <div className="mt-2 flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500">
                      <Icons.Clock className="mr-1" />
                      <span>Horaires: {point.hours}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-1 flex items-center text-sm text-gray-500">
                      <Icons.Phone className="mr-1" />
                      <span>{point.phone}</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow">
        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Suivi des livraisons</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="p-6">
          <div className="h-64 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-2">🗺️</div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Carte de suivi des livraisons en temps réel</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow">
        <div className="px-6 py-4 border-b border-gray-200">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Livreurs</h3>
        </div>
        <div className="p-6">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
            {mockData.couriers.map((courier) => (
              <div key={courier.id} className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center">
                  <div className="h-10 w-10 bg-gray-300 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                    <Icons.User />
                  </div>
                  <div className="ml-3">
                    <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">{courier.name}</h4>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{courier.vehicle}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 text-sm">
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Téléphone:</span>
                    <span className="ml-1">{courier.phone}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Livraisons:</span>
                    <span className="ml-1">{courier.deliveriesToday}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Note:</span>
                    <span className="ml-1">{courier.rating}/5</span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Statut:</span>
                    <span className={`ml-1 px-2 py-1 text-xs rounded-full ${getBadgeColor(courier.status)}`}>
                      {courier.status === 'active' ? 'Actif' : 'Inactif'}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  // Fonctionnalités avancées
  const AdvancedFeaturesTab = () => (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row justify-between items-start sm:items-center gap-4">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Fonctionnalités Avancées</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-600 mt-1">Systèmes intelligents pour améliorer votre plateforme</p>
        </div>
        <div className="relative">
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Rechercher..."
            value={searchQuery}
            onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
            className="pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 w-full sm:w-64"
          />
          <div className="absolute left-3 top-2.5 text-gray-400">
            <Icons.Search />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
          <div className="flex items-center mb-4">
            <div className="p-2 bg-blue-100 rounded-lg mr-3">
              <Icons.Brain />
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Intelligence Artificielle</h3>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Recommandations personnalisées</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Taux de conversion: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.recommendations.conversionRate}%</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Revenus générés: {formatCurrency(mockData.advancedAnalytics.recommendations.revenueGenerated)}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Détection de fraude</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Transactions détectées: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.fraudDetection.flaggedTransactions}</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Pertes évitées: {formatCurrency(mockData.advancedAnalytics.fraudDetection.preventedLosses)}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Chatbot de support</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Taux de résolution: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.chatbot.resolutionRate}%</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Temps moyen: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.chatbot.averageResponseTime}s</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
          <div className="flex items-center mb-4">
            <div className="p-2 bg-purple-100 rounded-lg mr-3">
              <Icons.Gift />
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">Marketing & Fidélité</h3>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Programme de fidélité</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Membres: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.loyalty.totalMembers}</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Taux de rétention: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.loyalty.retentionRate}%</p>
            </div>
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Système de parrainage</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Revenus générés: {formatCurrency(mockData.advancedAnalytics.referrals.revenueGenerated)}</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Taux de conversion: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.referrals.conversionRate}%</p>
            </div>
            <div className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-4">
              <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">Analytics & Suivi</h4>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">Visiteurs: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.totalVisitors.toLocaleString()}</p>
              <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Taux de conversion: {mockData.advancedAnalytics.conversionRate}%</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-6">
        <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-4">Analytics & Performance</h3>
        <div className="h-64 bg-gray-50 rounded flex items-center justify-center">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="text-4xl mb-2">📊</div>
            <p className="text-gray-500">Tableau de bord des performances</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  // Sidebar
  const Sidebar = () => (
    <div className={`fixed inset-y-0 left-0 z-50 w-64 bg-gray-900 text-white transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'translate-x-0' : '-translate-x-full'} lg:translate-x-0 lg:static lg:inset-0`}>
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between h-16 px-4 border-b border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mr-2">
            <span className="text-white font-bold text-sm">J</span>
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold">Jaay-ma Admin</span>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}
          className="lg:hidden"
        >
          <Icons.X />
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <nav className="mt-5 px-2">
        <div className="space-y-1">
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('dashboard'); setCurrentSection('dashboard'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'dashboard' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Dashboard />
            <span className="ml-3">Tableau de bord</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('products'); setCurrentSection('products'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'products' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Products />
            <span className="ml-3">Produits</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('users'); setCurrentSection('users'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'users' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Users />
            <span className="ml-3">Utilisateurs</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('orders'); setCurrentSection('orders'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'orders' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Orders />
            <span className="ml-3">Commandes</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('reviews'); setCurrentSection('reviews'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'reviews' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Reviews />
            <span className="ml-3">Avis</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('logistics'); setCurrentSection('logistics'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'logistics' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Truck />
            <span className="ml-3">Logistique</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('advanced'); setCurrentSection('advanced'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'advanced' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Brain />
            <span className="ml-3">Fonctionnalités avancées</span>
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={() => {setActiveTab('settings'); setCurrentSection('settings'); setSubSection(null);}}
            className={`w-full flex items-center px-2 py-2 text-sm rounded-md ${
              currentSection === 'settings' ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-300 hover:bg-gray-700 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            <Icons.Settings />
            <span className="ml-3">Paramètres</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </nav>
      
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 w-full p-4 border-t border-gray-700">
        <div className="flex items-center">
          <div className="h-8 w-8 bg-gray-300 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
            <Icons.User />
          </div>
          <div className="ml-3">
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{currentUser?.role}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleLogout}
          className="mt-3 w-full bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded text-sm"
        >
          Déconnexion
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  // Rendu du tableau actif
  const renderActiveTab = () => {
    switch (currentSection) {
      case 'dashboard':
        return <DashboardTab />;
      case 'products':
        return <ProductsTab />;
      case 'users':
        return <UsersTab />;
      case 'orders':
        return <OrdersTab />;
      case 'reviews':
        return <ReviewsTab />;
      case 'logistics':
        return <LogisticsTab />;
      case 'advanced':
        return <AdvancedFeaturesTab />;
      case 'settings':
        return <SettingsTab />;
      default:
        return <DashboardTab />;
    }
  };

  if (!currentUser || currentUser.role !== 'admin') {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="bg-white p-8 rounded-lg shadow-lg max-w-md w-full">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-gradient-to-r from-green-500 via-yellow-400 to-red-500 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
              <span className="text-white font-bold text-xl">J</span>
            </div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-4">Accès au panel administrateur</h2>
            <p className="text-gray-600 mb-6">Veuillez vous connecter avec un compte administrateur.</p>
            
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                <p><strong>Email:</strong> admin@jaay-ma.com</p>
                <p><strong>Mot de passe:</strong> n'importe lequel</p>
              </div>
              
              <input
                type="email"
                placeholder="Email"
                value={loginForm.email}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, email: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <input
                type="password"
                placeholder="Mot de passe"
                value={loginForm.password}
                onChange={(e) => setLoginForm({...loginForm, password: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-md focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500"
              />
              
              <button
                onClick={handleLogin}
                className="w-full bg-blue-500 hover:bg-blue-600 text-white py-2 px-4 rounded-lg font-medium"
              >
                Se connecter
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <AppContext.Provider value={{
      currentUser,
      cart,
      wishlist,
      notifications,
      addToCart,
      removeFromCart,
      updateCartItemQuantity,
      addToWishlist,
      removeFromWishlist,
      markNotificationAsRead
    }}>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-100">
        <Sidebar />
        
        <div className={`transition-all duration-300 ${sidebarOpen ? 'lg:ml-64' : 'lg:ml-0'} min-h-screen`}>
          <header className="bg-white shadow-sm border-b border-gray-200">
            <div className="px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-center">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(!sidebarOpen)}
                  className="lg:hidden p-2 rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100"
                >
                  <Icons.Menu />
                </button>
                <h1 className="ml-2 text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">
                  {currentSection === 'dashboard' && 'Tableau de bord'}
                  {currentSection === 'products' && 'Gestion des produits'}
                  {currentSection === 'users' && 'Gestion des utilisateurs'}
                  {currentSection === 'orders' && 'Gestion des commandes'}
                  {currentSection === 'reviews' && 'Modération des avis'}
                  {currentSection === 'logistics' && 'Logistique & Livraison'}
                  {currentSection === 'advanced' && 'Fonctionnalités avancées'}
                  {currentSection === 'settings' && 'Paramètres du système'}
                </h1>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex items-center space-x-4">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setShowCart(!showCart)}
                  className="relative p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                >
                  <Icons.Cart />
                  {cart.length > 0 && (
                    <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 bg-red-500 text-white text-xs rounded-full h-5 w-5 flex items-center justify-center">
                      {getTotalCartItems()}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </button>
                
                <button
                  onClick={() => setShowWishlist(!showWishlist)}
                  className="p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                >
                  <Icons.Wishlist />
                </button>
                
                <button
                  onClick={() => setShowNotifications(!showNotifications)}
                  className="relative p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                >
                  <Icons.Notification />
                  {notifications.filter(n => !n.read).length > 0 && (
                    <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 bg-red-500 text-white text-xs rounded-full h-5 w-5 flex items-center justify-center">
                      {notifications.filter(n => !n.read).length}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </button>
                
                <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">
                  Bienvenue, <span className="font-medium">{currentUser?.name}</span>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={handleLogout}
                  className="text-sm text-red-600 hover:text-red-800"
                >
                  Déconnexion
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </header>
          
          <main className="px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 min-h-screen">
            {renderActiveTab()}
          </main>
        </div>

        {/* Cart Sidebar */}
        {showCart && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-500 bg-opacity-75 transition-opacity" onClick={() => setShowCart(false)}></div>
            <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="pointer-events-none fixed inset-y-0 right-0 flex max-w-full pl-10">
                  <div className="pointer-events-auto w-screen max-w-md">
                    <div className="flex h-full flex-col overflow-y-scroll bg-white shadow-xl">
                      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-6 sm:px-6">
                        <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                          <h2 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900">Votre panier</h2>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => setShowCart(false)}
                            className="ml-3 flex h-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                          >
                            <Icons.X />
                          </button>
                        </div>

                        <div className="mt-8">
                          <div className="flow-root">
                            {cart.length === 0 ? (
                              <div className="text-center py-8">
                                <p className="text-gray-500">Votre panier est vide</p>
                              </div>
                            ) : (
                              <ul className="-my-6 divide-y divide-gray-200">
                                {cart.map((item) => (
                                  <li key={item.productId} className="flex py-6">
                                    <div className="h-24 w-24 flex-shrink-0 overflow-hidden rounded-md border border-gray-200">
                                      <img src={item.image} alt={item.name} className="h-full w-full object-cover object-center" />
                                    </div>

                                    <div className="ml-4 flex flex-1 flex-col">
                                      <div>
                                        <div className="flex justify-between text-base font-medium text-gray-900">
                                          <h3>{item.name}</h3>
                                          <p className="ml-4">{formatCurrency(item.price)}</p>
                                        </div>
                                        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-500">{item.seller}</p>
                                      </div>
                                      <div className="flex flex-1 items-end justify-between text-sm">
                                        <div className="flex items-center">
                                          <button
                                            onClick={() => updateCartItemQuantity(item.productId, item.quantity - 1)}
                                            className="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-600"
                                          >
                                            -
                                          </button>
                                          <p className="mx-2">{item.quantity}</p>
                                          <button
                                            onClick={() => updateCartItemQuantity(item.productId, item.quantity + 1)}
                                            className="text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-600"
                                          >
                                            +
                                          </button>
                                        </div>

                                        <button
                                          onClick={() => removeFromCart(item.productId)}
                                          className="font-medium text-red-600 hover:text-red-500"
                                        >
                                          Supprimer
                                        </button>
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </li>
                                ))}
                              </ul>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      {cart.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="border-t border-gray-200 px-4 py-6 sm:px-6">
                          <div className="flex justify-between text-base font-medium text-gray-900">
                            <p>Sous-total</p>
                            <p>{formatCurrency(getTotalCartValue())}</p>
                          </div>
                          <p className="mt-0.5 text-sm text-gray-500">Les frais de livraison seront calculés à la commande.</p>
                          <div className="mt-6">
                            <button
                              onClick={() => {
                                setShowCart(false);
                                setActiveTab('orders');
                              }}
                              className="w-full flex items-center justify-center rounded-md border border-transparent bg-blue-600 px-6 py-3 text-base font-medium text-white shadow-sm hover:bg-blue-700"
                            >
                              Passer la commande
                            </button>
                          </div>
                          <div className="mt-6 flex justify-center text-center text-sm text-gray-500">
                            <p>
                              ou{' '}
                              <button
                                type="button"
                                className="font-medium text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-500"
                                onClick={() => setShowCart(false)}
                              >
                                Continuer vos achats
                                <span aria-hidden="true"> &rarr;</span>
                              </button>
                            </p>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Wishlist Sidebar */}
        {showWishlist && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-500 bg-opacity-75 transition-opacity" onClick={() => setShowWishlist(false)}></div>
            <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="pointer-events-none fixed inset-y-0 right-0 flex max-w-full pl-10">
                  <div className="pointer-events-auto w-screen max-w-md">
                    <div className="flex h-full flex-col overflow-y-scroll bg-white shadow-xl">
                      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-6 sm:px-6">
                        <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                          <h2 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900">Votre liste de souhaits</h2>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => setShowWishlist(false)}
                            className="ml-3 flex h-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                          >
                            <Icons.X />
                          </button>
                        </div>

                        <div className="mt-8">
                          <div className="flow-root">
                            {wishlist.length === 0 ? (
                              <div className="text-center py-8">
                                <p className="text-gray-500">Votre liste de souhaits est vide</p>
                              </div>
                            ) : (
                              <ul className="-my-6 divide-y divide-gray-200">
                                {wishlist.map((item) => (
                                  <li key={item.productId} className="flex py-6">
                                    <div className="h-24 w-24 flex-shrink-0 overflow-hidden rounded-md border border-gray-200">
                                      <img src={item.image} alt={item.name} className="h-full w-full object-cover object-center" />
                                    </div>

                                    <div className="ml-4 flex flex-1 flex-col">
                                      <div>
                                        <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{item.name}</h3>
                                        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-gray-500">{item.category}</p>
                                      </div>
                                      <div className="flex flex-1 items-end justify-between text-sm">
                                        <p className="text-gray-900">{formatCurrency(item.price)}</p>

                                        <button
                                          onClick={() => removeFromWishlist(item.productId)}
                                          className="font-medium text-red-600 hover:text-red-500"
                                        >
                                          Supprimer
                                        </button>
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </li>
                                ))}
                              </ul>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Notifications Sidebar */}
        {showNotifications && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-500 bg-opacity-75 transition-opacity" onClick={() => setShowNotifications(false)}></div>
            <div className="fixed inset-0 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="absolute inset-0 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="pointer-events-none fixed inset-y-0 right-0 flex max-w-full pl-10">
                  <div className="pointer-events-auto w-screen max-w-md">
                    <div className="flex h-full flex-col overflow-y-scroll bg-white shadow-xl">
                      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-6 sm:px-6">
                        <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                          <h2 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900">Notifications</h2>
                          <button
                            onClick={() => setShowNotifications(false)}
                            className="ml-3 flex h-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-500"
                          >
                            <Icons.X />
                          </button>
                        </div>

                        <div className="mt-8">
                          <div className="flow-root">
                            {notifications.length === 0 ? (
                              <div className="text-center py-8">
                                <p className="text-gray-500">Aucune notification</p>
                              </div>
                            ) : (
                              <ul className="-my-6 divide-y divide-gray-200">
                                {notifications.map((notification) => (
                                  <li key={notification.id} className={`py-6 ${!notification.read ? 'bg-blue-50' : ''}`}>
                                    <div className="flex">
                                      <div className="ml-4 flex-1">
                                        <p className={`text-sm ${!notification.read ? 'font-medium text-blue-900' : 'text-gray-900'}`}>
                                          {notification.message}
                                        </p>
                                        <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500">{formatDate(notification.date)}</p>
                                        {!notification.read && (
                                          <button
                                            onClick={() => markNotificationAsRead(notification.id)}
                                            className="mt-2 text-xs text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-500"
                                          >
                                            Marquer comme lu
                                          </button>
                                        )}
                                      </div>
                                    </div>
                                  </li>
                                ))}
                              </ul>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </AppContext.Provider>
  );
};

export default App;
